@$mol_mem
dependent_source( next?: string ): string {
const old_value = $mol_wire_probe( () => this.dependent_source() )
if( next === undefined) {
const value = this.value()
if( old_value !== value ) {
this.value_moment( new $mol_time_moment(value) )
return value
} else {
const moment_str = this.value_moment().toString( 'YYYY-MM-DD hh:mm' )
this.value( moment_str )
return moment_str
}
}
this.value_moment( new $mol_time_moment(next) )
this.value(next)
return next
